Structural Schema Extraction**\\nThe `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apiserver/schema/convert.go` implements `NewStructural()` which converts JSONSchemaProps to a structural schema representation (defined in `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apiserver/schema/structural.go`). Structural schemas enforce Kubernetes' stricter validation invariants and are required for many features including field management and pruning.\\n\\n**4. Structural Schema to OpenAPI v3 Conversion**\\nThe `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apiserver/schema/kubeopenapi.go` file implements the `ToKubeOpenAPI()` method on the Structural type, which converts the internal structural representation back to the standard go-openapi spec.Schema format for publication.\\n\\n**5. OpenAPI Controller (Dynamic Spec Management)**\\nThe `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/controller/openapi/controller.go` implements the OpenAPI controller which:\\n- Watches CustomResourceDefinition changes via informers\\n- Builds merged OpenAPI v2 specs for all served CRD versions\\n- Lazily constructs and caches specs per CRD\\n- Updates the OpenAPIService to publish updated specs\\n\\nThe OpenAPI v3 controller is implemented in `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/controller/openapiv3/controller.go` with similar functionality.\\n\\n**7.
